```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:

    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

| blk-27-2 | 119 | 5259 | para |
| blk-27-3 | 363 | 4621 | code |
| blk-27-4 | 58 | 718 | table |

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```javascript
function processChunk(id, data) {
  const filtered = data.filter(x => x.enabled && x.score > 0.5);
  return filtered.map(x => ({ id, value: x.score * x.weight }));
}
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:

    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:

```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
```

```python
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

> **Note 161:** Estimate virtual viewport fence reference sync block fence buffer codemirror. Measure document buffer buffer measure heading block block heading block buffer footnote split document document. Leader layout document split codemirror experimental viewport footnote split pane experimental estimate.

Inline mix: **bold**, *italic*, `inline code`, and [link #161](#section-161-mixed-content-block).

```python
def merge_blocks(blocks, threshold=320):
    out = []
    for b in blocks:
        if len(out) and len(out[-1]) + len(b) < threshold:
            out[-1] += b
        else:
            out.append(b)
    return out
```

```javascript
function processChunk(id, data) {
  const filtered = data.filter(x => x.enabled && x.score > 0.5);
  return filtered.map(x => ({ id, value: x.score * x.weight }));
}
```

```sql
FROM markdown_blocks
WHERE document_id = $1
```
